<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.12.0">0.12.0</a> - 2023-11-26</h2><a id="user-content-0120---2023-11-26" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.12.0 - 2023-11-26" href="#0120---2023-11-26"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">💥 <strong>Breaking changes</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Minimum PHP version is now 8.1</li>
<li><code>RoundingMode</code> is now an <code>enum</code>; if you're type-hinting rounding modes, you need to type-hint against <code>RoundingMode</code> instead of <code>int</code> now</li>
<li><code>BigNumber</code> classes do not implement the <code>Serializable</code> interface anymore (they use the <a href="https://wiki.php.net/rfc/custom_object_serialization" rel="nofollow">new custom object serialization mechanism</a>)</li>
<li>The following breaking changes only affect you if you're creating your own <code>BigNumber</code> subclasses:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the return type of <code>BigNumber::of()</code> is now <code>static</code></li>
<li><code>BigNumber</code> has a new abstract method <code>from()</code></li>
<li>all <code>public</code> and <code>protected</code> functions of <code>BigNumber</code> are now <code>final</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.11.0">0.11.0</a> - 2023-01-16</h2><a id="user-content-0110---2023-01-16" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.11.0 - 2023-01-16" href="#0110---2023-01-16"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">💥 <strong>Breaking changes</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Minimum PHP version is now 8.0</li>
<li>Methods accepting a union of types are now strongly typed<sup>*</sup></li>
<li><code>MathException</code> now extends <code>Exception</code> instead of <code>RuntimeException</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><sup>* You may now run into type errors if you were passing <code>Stringable</code> objects to <code>of()</code> or any of the methods
internally calling <code>of()</code>, with <code>strict_types</code> enabled. You can fix this by casting <code>Stringable</code> objects to <code>string</code>
first.</sup></p>

</ul>

<li>Deprecated method <code>BigInteger::parse()</code> has been removed - use <code>fromBase()</code> instead</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.8.16">0.8.16</a> - 2020-08-18</h2><a id="user-content-0816---2020-08-18" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.8.16 - 2020-08-18" href="#0816---2020-08-18"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">🚑 <strong>Critical fix</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>This version reintroduces the deprecated <code>BigInteger::parse()</code> method, that has been removed by mistake in version <code>0.8.9</code> and should have lasted for the whole <code>0.8</code> release cycle.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">✨ <strong>New features</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>BigInteger::modInverse()</code> calculates a modular multiplicative inverse</li>
<li><code>BigInteger::fromBytes()</code> creates a <code>BigInteger</code> from a byte string</li>
<li><code>BigInteger::toBytes()</code> converts a <code>BigInteger</code> to a byte string</li>
<li><code>BigInteger::randomBits()</code> creates a pseudo-random <code>BigInteger</code> of a given bit length</li>
<li><code>BigInteger::randomRange()</code> creates a pseudo-random <code>BigInteger</code> between two bounds</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">💩 <strong>Deprecations</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>BigInteger::powerMod()</code> is now deprecated in favour of <code>modPow()</code></li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.8.9">0.8.9</a> - 2020-01-08</h2><a id="user-content-089---2020-01-08" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.8.9 - 2020-01-08" href="#089---2020-01-08"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.8.8">0.8.8</a> - 2019-04-25</h2><a id="user-content-088---2019-04-25" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.8.8 - 2019-04-25" href="#088---2019-04-25"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">🐛 <strong>Bug fixes</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>BigInteger::toBase()</code> could return an empty string for zero values (BCMath &amp; Native calculators only, GMP calculator unaffected)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">✨ <strong>New features</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>BigInteger::toArbitraryBase()</code> converts a number to an arbitrary base, using a custom alphabet</li>
<li><code>BigInteger::fromArbitraryBase()</code> converts a string in an arbitrary base, using a custom alphabet, back to a number</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">These methods can be used as the foundation to convert strings between different bases/alphabets, using BigInteger as an intermediate representation.</p>
<p dir="auto">💩 <strong>Deprecations</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>BigInteger::parse()</code> is now deprecated in favour of <code>fromBase()</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><code>BigInteger::fromBase()</code> works the same way as <code>parse()</code>, with 2 minor differences:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the <code>$base</code> parameter is required, it does not default to <code>10</code></li>
<li>it throws a <code>NumberFormatException</code> instead of an <code>InvalidArgumentException</code> when the number is malformed</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.8.7">0.8.7</a> - 2019-04-20</h2><a id="user-content-087---2019-04-20" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.8.7 - 2019-04-20" href="#087---2019-04-20"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Improvements</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Safer conversion from <code>float</code> when using custom locales</li>
<li><strong>Much faster</strong> <code>NativeCalculator</code> implementation 🚀</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">You can expect <strong>at least a 3x performance improvement</strong> for common arithmetic operations when using the library on systems without GMP or BCMath; it gets exponentially faster on multiplications with a high number of digits. This is due to calculations now being performed on whole blocks of digits (the block size depending on the platform, 32-bit or 64-bit) instead of digit-by-digit as before.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.8.6">0.8.6</a> - 2019-04-11</h2><a id="user-content-086---2019-04-11" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.8.6 - 2019-04-11" href="#086---2019-04-11"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<p dir="auto"><code>BigNumber::sum()</code> returns the sum of one or more numbers.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.8.3">0.8.3</a> - 2018-12-06</h2><a id="user-content-083---2018-12-06" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.8.3 - 2018-12-06" href="#083---2018-12-06"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>New method</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>BigInteger::sqrt()</code> calculates the square root of a number (thanks @peter279k).</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>New exception</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>NegativeNumberException</code> is thrown when calling <code>sqrt()</code> on a negative number.</p>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Breaking changes</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The following deprecated methods have been removed. Use the new method name instead:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Method removed</th>
<th>Replacement method</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>BigDecimal::getIntegral()</code></td>
<td><code>BigDecimal::getIntegralPart()</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>BigDecimal::getFraction()</code></td>
<td><code>BigDecimal::getFractionalPart()</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<hr>
<p dir="auto"><strong>New features</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>BigInteger</code> has been augmented with 5 new methods for bitwise operations:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>New method</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>and()</code></td>
<td>performs a bitwise <code>AND</code> operation on two numbers</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>or()</code></td>
<td>performs a bitwise <code>OR</code> operation on two numbers</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>xor()</code></td>
<td>performs a bitwise <code>XOR</code> operation on two numbers</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>shiftedLeft()</code></td>
<td>returns the number shifted left by a number of bits</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>shiftedRight()</code></td>
<td>returns the number shifted right by a number of bits</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto">Thanks to @DASPRiD 👍</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.5.4">0.5.4</a> - 2016-10-17</h2><a id="user-content-054---2016-10-17" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.5.4 - 2016-10-17" href="#054---2016-10-17"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.5.3">0.5.3</a> - 2016-03-31</h2><a id="user-content-053---2016-03-31" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.5.3 - 2016-03-31" href="#053---2016-03-31"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This is a bugfix release. Dividing by a negative power of 1 with the same scale as the dividend could trigger an incorrect optimization which resulted in a wrong result. See #6.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.5.2">0.5.2</a> - 2015-08-06</h2><a id="user-content-052---2015-08-06" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.5.2 - 2015-08-06" href="#052---2015-08-06"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>$scale</code> parameter of <code>BigDecimal::dividedBy()</code> is now optional again.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.5.1">0.5.1</a> - 2015-07-05</h2><a id="user-content-051---2015-07-05" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.5.1 - 2015-07-05" href="#051---2015-07-05"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>New method: <code>BigNumber::toScale()</code></strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This allows to convert any <code>BigNumber</code> to a <code>BigDecimal</code> with a given scale, using rounding if necessary.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.5.0">0.5.0</a> - 2015-07-04</h2><a id="user-content-050---2015-07-04" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.5.0 - 2015-07-04" href="#050---2015-07-04"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>New features</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Common <code>BigNumber</code> interface for all classes, with the following methods:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>sign()</code> and derived methods (<code>isZero()</code>, <code>isPositive()</code>, ...)</li>
<li><code>compareTo()</code> and derived methods (<code>isEqualTo()</code>, <code>isGreaterThan()</code>, ...) that work across different <code>BigNumber</code> types</li>
<li><code>toBigInteger()</code>, <code>toBigDecimal()</code>, <code>toBigRational</code>() conversion methods</li>
<li><code>toInteger()</code> and <code>toFloat()</code> conversion methods to native types</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Unified <code>of()</code> behaviour: every class now accepts any type of number, provided that it can be safely converted to the current type</li>
<li>New method: <code>BigDecimal::exactlyDividedBy()</code>; this method automatically computes the scale of the result, provided that the division yields a finite number of digits</li>
<li>New methods: <code>BigRational::quotient()</code> and <code>remainder()</code></li>
<li>Fine-grained exceptions: <code>DivisionByZeroException</code>, <code>RoundingNecessaryException</code>, <code>NumberFormatException</code></li>
<li>Factory methods <code>zero()</code>, <code>one()</code> and <code>ten()</code> available in all classes</li>
<li>Rounding mode reintroduced in <code>BigInteger::dividedBy()</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">This release also comes with many performance improvements.</p>
<hr>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Breaking changes</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>BigInteger</code>:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>getSign()</code> is renamed to <code>sign()</code></li>
<li><code>toString()</code> is renamed to <code>toBase()</code></li>
<li><code>BigInteger::dividedBy()</code> now throws an exception by default if the remainder is not zero; use <code>quotient()</code> to get the previous behaviour</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>BigDecimal</code>:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>getSign()</code> is renamed to <code>sign()</code></li>
<li><code>getUnscaledValue()</code> is renamed to <code>unscaledValue()</code></li>
<li><code>getScale()</code> is renamed to <code>scale()</code></li>
<li><code>getIntegral()</code> is renamed to <code>integral()</code></li>
<li><code>getFraction()</code> is renamed to <code>fraction()</code></li>
<li><code>divideAndRemainder()</code> is renamed to <code>quotientAndRemainder()</code></li>
<li><code>dividedBy()</code> now takes a <strong>mandatory</strong> <code>$scale</code> parameter <strong>before</strong> the rounding mode</li>
<li><code>toBigInteger()</code> does not accept a <code>$roundingMode</code> parameter anymore</li>
<li><code>toBigRational()</code> does not simplify the fraction anymore; explicitly add <code>-&gt;simplified()</code> to get the previous behaviour</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>BigRational</code>:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>getSign()</code> is renamed to <code>sign()</code></li>
<li><code>getNumerator()</code> is renamed to  <code>numerator()</code></li>
<li><code>getDenominator()</code> is renamed to  <code>denominator()</code></li>
<li><code>of()</code> is renamed to <code>nd()</code>, while <code>parse()</code> is renamed to <code>of()</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Miscellaneous:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>ArithmeticException</code> is moved to an <code>Exception\</code> sub-namespace</li>
<li><code>of()</code> factory methods now throw <code>NumberFormatException</code> instead of <code>InvalidArgumentException</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.4.3">0.4.3</a> - 2016-03-31</h2><a id="user-content-043---2016-03-31" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.4.3 - 2016-03-31" href="#043---2016-03-31"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Backport of two bug fixes from the 0.5 branch:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>BigInteger::parse()</code> did not always throw <code>InvalidArgumentException</code> as expected</li>
<li>Dividing by a negative power of 1 with the same scale as the dividend could trigger an incorrect optimization which resulted in a wrong result. See #6.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.4.2">0.4.2</a> - 2015-06-16</h2><a id="user-content-042---2015-06-16" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.4.2 - 2015-06-16" href="#042---2015-06-16"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">New method: <code>BigDecimal::stripTrailingZeros()</code></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.4.1">0.4.1</a> - 2015-06-12</h2><a id="user-content-041---2015-06-12" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.4.1 - 2015-06-12" href="#041---2015-06-12"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Introducing a <code>BigRational</code> class, to perform calculations on fractions of any size.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.4.0">0.4.0</a> - 2015-06-12</h2><a id="user-content-040---2015-06-12" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.4.0 - 2015-06-12" href="#040---2015-06-12"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Rounding modes have been removed from <code>BigInteger</code>, and are now a concept specific to <code>BigDecimal</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>BigInteger::dividedBy()</code> now always returns the quotient of the division.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.3.5">0.3.5</a> - 2016-03-31</h2><a id="user-content-035---2016-03-31" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.3.5 - 2016-03-31" href="#035---2016-03-31"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<ul dir="auto">

</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.3.2">0.3.2</a> - 2015-06-07</h2><a id="user-content-032---2015-06-07" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.3.2 - 2015-06-07" href="#032---2015-06-07"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>BigInteger</code> and <code>BigDecimal</code> now have a <code>getSign()</code> method that returns:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>-1</code> if the number is negative</li>
<li><code>0</code> if the number is zero</li>
<li><code>1</code> if the number is positive</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.3.1">0.3.1</a> - 2015-06-05</h2><a id="user-content-031---2015-06-05" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.3.1 - 2015-06-05" href="#031---2015-06-05"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Minor performance improvements</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.3.0">0.3.0</a> - 2015-06-04</h2><a id="user-content-030---2015-06-04" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.3.0 - 2015-06-04" href="#030---2015-06-04"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>$roundingMode</code> and <code>$scale</code> parameters have been swapped in <code>BigDecimal::dividedBy()</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.2.2">0.2.2</a> - 2015-06-04</h2><a id="user-content-022---2015-06-04" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.2.2 - 2015-06-04" href="#022---2015-06-04"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Stronger immutability guarantee for <code>BigInteger</code> and <code>BigDecimal</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">So far, it would have been possible to break immutability of these classes by calling the <code>unserialize()</code> internal function. This release fixes that.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.2.1">0.2.1</a> - 2015-06-02</h2><a id="user-content-021---2015-06-02" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.2.1 - 2015-06-02" href="#021---2015-06-02"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Added <code>BigDecimal::divideAndRemainder()</code></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/brick/math/releases/tag/0.2.0">0.2.0</a> - 2015-05-22</h2><a id="user-content-020---2015-05-22" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.2.0 - 2015-05-22" href="#020---2015-05-22"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
